				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Schwingt freudig euch empor, BWV 36 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 (early version) or 8 (revised version)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725-1730, rev. 1731
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Schwingt freudig euch empor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Soar joyfully upwards
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="it">Schwingt freudig euch empor BWV 36</span>; <span title="ja">喜びて舞いあがれ</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/184268105">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Schwingt_freudig_euch_empor,_BWV_36">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/184268105">184268105</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300007175">300007175</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13981483n">13981483n</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 36&#160;; BC A 3a-b
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 579
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 (early version) or 8 movements in 2 parts (revised version):
<ul><li><b>Early Version (1725-30)</b>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>1. Chorus: Schwingt freudig euch empor (D major)
</dd><dd>2. Aria (Tenor): Die Liebe zieht mit sanften Schritten (B minor)
</dd><dd>3. Aria (bass): Willkommen, werter Schatz (D major), 55 measures
</dd><dd>4. Aria (Soprano): Auch mit gedämpften, schwachen Stimmen (A major)
</dd><dd>5. Chorale: Wie bin ich doch so herzlich froh (D major)
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>Revised Version (1731)</b>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Prima Pars</i>
<dl><dd>1. Chorus: Schwingt freudig euch empor (D major)
</dd><dd>2. Choral: Nun komm, der Heiden Heiland (F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span> minor)
</dd><dd>3. Aria (Tenor): Die Liebe zieht mit sanften Schritten (B minor)
</dd><dd>4. Chorale: Zwingt die Saiten in Cythara (D major)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Secunda Pars</i>
<dl><dd>5. Aria (bass): Willkommen, werter Schatz (D major)
</dd><dd>6. Chorale (Tenor): Der du bist dem Vater gleich (B minor)
</dd><dd>7. Aria (Soprano): Auch mit gedämpften, schwachen Stimmen (G major)
</dd><dd>8. Chorale: Lob sei Gott dem Vater ton (B minor)
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1725-1730, rev. 1731
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1725-1730, rev. 1731-12-2 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1857 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>

</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

</th>

</td></tr>

</li><li> BWV 220: <i><a href="/wiki/Lobt_ihn_mit_Herz_und_Munde,_BWV_220_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Lobt ihn mit Herz und Munde, BWV 220 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Lobt ihn mit Herz und Munde</a></i> (composer unknown)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
